SKYABS YIN TE, RKANG GNYIS RNAMS KYI MCHOG YIN PA'I PHYIR RO ZHES
BSTAN ZHING RNAM PAR GZHAG GO, ,STON PA'I YON TAN BSTAN PA'I DON
DU, RANG NYID RTEN 'BREL GYI CHOS ZAB MO RJES SU RTOGS PA'I PHYIR
ZHUGS PA, RANG SANGS RGYAS KYI THEG PA PA'I GANG ZAG DANG, CHOS

LA MCHOG TU BYA BA BYED PAR MOS PA RNAMS KYI DBANG DU BYAS NAS
CHOS NI SKYABS YIN TE, 'DOD CHAGS DANG BRAL BA RNAMS KYI MCHOG
YIN PA'I PHYIR RO ZHES BSTAN ZHING RNAM PAR GZHAG GO, ,STON PA'I
BSTAN PA LA LEGS PAR ZHUGS PA'I SLOB MA'I YON TAN BSTAN PA'I DON
DU

GZHAN LAS THOS PA'I SGRA'I RJES SU RTOGS PA'I PHYIR ZHUGS PA'I
NYAN THOS KYI THEG PA'I GANG ZAG DANG, DGE 'DUN LA MCHOG TU BYA
BA BYED PAR MOS PA RNAMS KYI DBANG DU BYAS NAS DGE 'DUN NI SKYABS
YIN TE, TSOGS RNAMS KYI MCHOG YIN PA'I PHYIR RO ZHES BSTAN

@84A *, ,CING RNAM PAR GZHAG GO, ,DE LTAR 'DIS NI MDOR BSDU NA
DON RNAM PA GSUM GYIS GANG ZAG DRUG GI DBANG DU BYAS NAS, BCOM
LDAN 'DAS KYIS SKYABS GSUM RAB TU DBYE BA BSTAN PA RNAM PAR GZHAG
PA 'DI NI KUN RDZOB KYI RTEN LA GNAS PA SEMS CAN RNAMS

THEG PA LA RIM GYIS GZHUG PA'I DON DU YIN NO, ,SDANG PHYIR SLU
BA'I CHOS CAN PHYIR, ,MED PHYIR 'JIGS DANG BCAS PA'I PHYIR, ,CHOS
RNAMS GNYIS DANG 'PHAGS PA'I TSOGS, ,GTAN GYI SKYABS MCHOG MA YIN
NO, ,CHOS NI RNAM PAR GNYIS TE, BSTAN PA'I CHOS DANG RTOGS

PA'I CHOS SO, ,DE LTAR BSTAN PA'I CHOS NI MDO'I SDE LA SOGS PA
BSTAN PA BRJOD PA STE, MING DANG TSIG DANG YI GE'I TSOGS KYIS
BSDUS PA'O, ,DE YANG LAM MNGON PAR RTOGS PA'I MTHAR THUG PA'I
PHYIR GZINGS LTA BU'O ZHES BSHAD DO, ,RTOGS PA'I CHOS NI RGYU
DANG

'BRAS BU'I DBYE BA RNAM PA GNYIS TE, 'DI LTA STE, LAM GYI BDEN PA
DANG, 'GOG PA'I BDEN PA STE, GANG GIS DANG GANG RTOGS PA ZHES BYA
BAS SO, ,DE LA LAM NI 'DUS BYAS KYI MTSAN NYID DU RTOGS LA, 'DUS
BYAS KYI MTSAN NYID DU RTOGS PA GANG YIN PA

'DI NI BRDZUN PA SLU BA'I CHOS CAN GANG BRDZUN PA SLU BA'I CHOS
CHAN DE NI MI BDEN PA, GANG MI BDEN PA DE NI MI RTAG PA, GANG
MING RTAG PA DE NI SKYABS MA YIN NO, ,LAM DES RTOGS PA'I 'GOG PA
GANG YIN PA DE YANG NYAN THOS KYI TSUL GYIS MAR ME RGYUN CHAD PA
BZHIN DU NYON MONGS PA

DANG SDUG BSNGAL MED PA TZAM GYIS RAB TU PHYE LA, MED PA NI
SKYABS SAM SKYABS MA YIN PAR 'GYUR BAR 'OS PA MA YIN NO, ,DGE

TSIG BLA DAGS SO, ,DE YANG RTAG TU 'JIGS PA DANG BCAS PA DE BZHIN
GSHEGS

PA LA SKYABS SU SONG BA, NGES PAR 'BYUNG BA TSOL BA SLOB PA BYA

@84B CHAGS MA SPANGS PA'I PHYIR RTAG TU RGYUN MI 'CHAD PAR 'DU

DANG BSAM GTAN GNYIS DAG NI,

GANG, ,DE NI SHES BYA'I SGRIB PAR 'DOD, ,SER SNA LA SOGS RNAM
RTOG GANG, ,DE NI NYON MONGS SGRIB PAR 'DOD, ,SHES RAB LAS GZHAN
'DI DAG NI, ,SPONG RGYU GZHAN MED DE YI PHYIR, ,SHES RAB CHOG YIN
DE BZHI NI, ,

@128B THOS PA DE PHYIR THOS PA MCHOG, ,DE LTAR YIN CHES LUNG DANG
RIGS PA LA, ,BRTEN NAS BDAG NYID 'BA' ZHIG DAG PHYIR DANG, ,GANG
DAG MOS DGE PHUN SUM TSOGS LDAN BLO, ,DE DAG RJES SU GZUNG PHYIR
'DI BSHAD NGO, ,JI LTAR BSHAD PA 'DI LAS BRTZAMS TE TSIGS SU BCAD
PA, ,JI LTAR SGRON GLOG NOR BU

NYI ZLA LA, ,BRTEN NAS MIG DANG LDAN PA LTA BA BZHIN, ,DE BZHIN
DON CHEN CHOS SPOBS 'OD MDZAD PA, ,THUB LA BRTEN NAS 'DI NI RAB
TU BSHAD, ,GANG BSHAD PA DE LAS BRTZAMS TE TSIGS SU BCAD PA,
,GANG ZHIG DON LDAN CHOS DANG NYER 'BREL ZHING, ,KHAMS GSUM KUN
NAS NYON MONGS SPONG BYED GSUNG, ,

ZHI BA'I PHAN YON STON PAR MDZAD PA GANG, ,DE NI DRANG SRONG
GSUNG YIN BZLOG PA GZHAN, ,GANG GIS BSHAD PA DE LAS BRTZAMS TE
TSIGS SU BCAD PA, ,GANG ZHIG RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA 'BA' ZHIG GIS,
,DBANG BYAS RNAM G-YENG MED YID CAN GYIS BSHAD, ,THAR BA THOB
PA'I LAM DANG RJES

MTHUN PAR, ,DE YANG DRANG SROD BKA' BZHIN SPYI BOS BLANG, ,BDAG
BSRUNG BA'I THABS LAS BRTZAMS TE TSIGS SU BCAD PA, GANG PHYIR
RGYAL LAS CHES MKHAS 'GA' YANG 'JIG RTEN 'DI NA YOD MIN TE, ,MA
LUS DE NYID MCHOG TSUL BZHIN KUN MKHYEN GYIS MKHYEN GZHAN MIN PA,
,DE PHYIR

DRANG SRONG RANG NYID KYIS GZHAG MDO SDE GANG YIN DE MI DKRUG
,THUB TSUL GZHIG PHYIR DE YANG DAM CHOS LA NI GNOD PA BYED PAR
'GYUR, ,NYON MONGS RMONGS BDAG RNAMS KYIS 'PHAGS LA SKUR BA DANG,
,DES GSUNGS CHOS LA BRNYAS GANG DE KUN ZHEN LTAS BYAS, ,DES NA
ZHEN LTA'I DRI CAN DE LA BLO MI SBYAR,,

GOS GTZANG TSON GYIS RNAM BSGYUR SNUM GYIS GOS PA MIN, ,NYAMS
PA'I RGYU LAS BRTZAMS TE TSIGS SU BCAD PA, ,BLO DMAN PHYIR DANG
DKAR MOS BRAL PHYIR LOG PA'I NGA RGYAL BSTAN PHYIR DANG, ,DAM
CHOS PHONGS PAS BSGRIB PA'I BDAG PHYIR DRANG DON DE NYID 'DZIN
PA'I PHYIR, ,RNYED LA BRKAM PHYIR LTA

BA'I DBANG PHYIR CHOS SU 'BYIN PA BRTEN PHYIR DANG, ,CHOS 'DZIN
BSRINGS PHYIR MOS PA DMAN PHYIR DGRA BCOM RNAMS KYI CHOS SPONG
BYED, ,NYAMS PA'I 'BRAS BU LAS BRTZAMS TE TSIGS SU BCAD PA, ,JI
LTAR ZAB MO'I CHOS RNAMS DE BZHIN MKHAS PA RNAMS KYIS ME DANG NI,
,MI BZAD SBRUL GDUG GSHED

@129A *, ,MA DANG NI THOG LA'ANG SHIN TU 'JIGS MA BYI, ,ME SBRUL
DGRA DANG RDO RJE'I MES NI SROG DANG BRAL BRTZAM BYED DE, ,DE LAS
MNAR MED RNAMS KYI 'GRO BA SHIN TU 'JIGS PAR 'GRO MI 'GYUR, ,GANG
ZHIG YANG YANG SDIG GROGS BSTEN PAS SANGS RGYAS NGAN SEMS LDAN
GYUR DANG, ,PHAM DGRA BCOM GSOD

PA BYA BA MIN BYED MCHOG TSOGS 'BYED PA'I MI, ,DE YANG CHOS NYID
NGES PAR BSAMS PAS MYUR DU DE LAS THAR 'GYUR GYI, ,GANG ZHIG YID
NI CHOS LA SDANG BA DE LA THAR PA GA LA YOD, ,DKON MCHOG RNAM PAR
BYANG KHAMS DRI MED BYANG CHUB YON TAN PHRIN LAS TE, ,DON GNAS
RNAM BDUN TSUL BZHIN BSHAD LAS

BDAG GIS DGE BA GANG THOB PA, ,DES NI 'GRO 'DI MTHA' YAS 'OD MANG
DRANG SRONG TSE DPAG MED MTHONG ZHING, ,MTHONG NAS KYANG NI CHOS
MIG DRI MED SKYES TE BYANG CHUB MCHOG THOB SHOG, ,TSIGS SU BCAD
PA BCU BO 'DI DAG GIS BSDUS PA'I DON YANG TSIGS SU BCAD PA RNAM
PA GSUM GYIS RIG PAR BYA STE, ,GANG LAS

RGYU MTSAN GANG PHYIR NI, ,JI LTA BUR NI GANG BRJOD DANG, ,RGYU
MTHUN PA NI GNANG YIN DE, ,TSIGS SU BCAD PA BZHIS BSTAN TO,
,GNYIS KYI BDAG NYID DAG PA YI, ,THABS DANG GCIG GIS NYAMS BA'I
RGYU, ,DE NAS TSIGS SU BCAD PA NI, ,GNYIS KYIS 'BRAS BU BSTAN PA
YIN, ,'KHOR GYI DKYIL 'KHOR BZOD PA DANG, ,

BYANG CHUB THOB PA'I CHOS BRJOD PA'I, ,MDOR NA 'BRAS BU RNAM
GNYIS NI, ,THA MA YIS NI BSTAN PA YIN, ,THEG PA CHEN PO RGYUD BLA
MA'I BSTAN BCOS, ,DKON MCHOG GI RIGS RNAM PAR DBYE BA LAS PHAN
YON GYI LE'U STE LNGA BA'O,, ,,TSIGS SU BCAD PA'I DON GYIS BSDUS
BA'I BSHAD PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,

THEG MCHOG DAM CHOS RIN CHEN BSHAD 'DI LAS, ,BSAM YAS BSOD NAMS
BDAG GIS GANG THOB PA, ,DES NI 'GRO KUN THEG MCHOG DAM PA'I CHOS,
,RIN CHEN DRI MA MED PA'I SNOD GYUR CIG, ,'PHAGS PA MGON PO BYAMS
PAS MDZAD PA, ,THEG PA CHEN PO RGYUD BLA MA'I BSTAN BCOS KYI RNAM
PAR

BSHAD PA SLOB DPON THOGS MED KYIS MDZAD PA RDZOGS SO,, ,,DPAL
GRONG KHYER CHEN PO DPE MED KYI MKHAS PA CHEN PO BRAM ZE RIN CHEN
RDO RJE'I DBON PO, ,PAndI TA MKHAS PA CHEN PO SAD DZA NA DANG, LO
RTZA BA SH'AKYA'I DGE SLONG BLO LDAN SHES RAB KYIS, ,GRONG KHYER
DPE MED DE NYID DU BSGYUR BA'O,, ,,
